## The .gov means it's official. 
Local, state, and federal government websites often end in .gov. Commonwealth of Pennsylvania government websites and email systems use "pennsylvania.gov" or "pa.gov" at the end of the address. Before sharing sensitive or personal information, make sure you're on an official state website.

>www.dpw.state.pa.us > www.dhs.pa.gov 8/12/2025 3 • Treat the application seriously. It is a legal agreement and a signed attestation to comply with a vast array of federal and state Medicaid rules…it is far more than just getting a “billing number”. • Make sure your enrollers do good QC checks of your application content before submission. Minimize need to return apps for corrections and the associated delays. Your enrollers can and should check their app status in the portal. • If you/your enrollers have questions about revalidation or enrollment status, the best thing to do is contact MA enrollment staff at: 800-537-8862 Option 2 Option 4. >www.dpw.state.pa.us > www.dhs.pa.gov 8/12/2025 5 Policy UpdatesUpcoming MABs to be Issued After issuance the MABs in this section will be accessible at the following links respectively: What’s New at OMAP and Bulletin Search.
* * *
> “Adoption of the American Academy of Pediatric Dentistry’s Dental Periodicity Schedule” (TBD)
This bulletin advises providers that the Department of Human Services (Department) will adopt the American Academy of Pediatric Dentistry (AAPD)’s dental periodicity schedule to replace the Department’s Dental Periodicity Schedule. The Dental Periodicity Schedule was last updated with Medical Assistance (MA) Bulletin 27-13-15, titled “2023 Pediatric Dental Periodicity Schedule Updates” that was issued on 10/3/23.
* * *
> “Prior Authorization Guidelines for Enteral Nutrition” (TBD)
This bulletin advises providers of the guidelines for prior authorization to support the medical necessity of prescriptions for enteral nutrition. This bulletin is also to issue new provider handbook pages that include the requirements for prior authorization and the information to evaluate the medical necessity of prescriptions for enteral nutrition. Effective July 18, 2025, the Department uses Milliman Care Guidelines (MCG) to determine medical necessity for services, items, procedures, or level of care provided to MA beneficiaries. There are no MCG guidelines for enteral nutrition. Therefore, the Department is advising providers of the clinical guidelines to be utilized for prior authorization of enteral nutrition for MA beneficiaries.
* * *
> “Prior Authorization Guidelines for Wearable Air Conduction Hearing Aids” (TBD)
This bulletin advises providers of the guidelines for prior authorization to support the medical necessity of prescriptions for wearable air conduction hearing aids. This bulletin is also to issue new provider handbook pages that include the requirements for prior authorization and the information needed to evaluate the medical necessity of prescriptions for wearable air conduction hearing aids. Effective July 18, 2025, the Department uses MCG to determine medical necessity for services, items, procedures, or level of care provided to MA beneficiaries. There are no MCG guidelines for wearable air conduction hearing aids. Therefore, the Department is advising providers of the clinical guidelines to be utilized for prior authorization of wearable air conduction hearing aids for MA beneficiaries. These guidelines apply to wearable air conduction hearing aids only.
* * *
